    const themeList = ['green', 'red', 'blue', 'yellow'];
    const theme = localStorage.getItem('theme') || themeList[1];
    const themeMap = {
        green: '绿色主题',
        red: '红色主题',
        blue: '蓝色主题',
        yellow: '橙色主题',

        theme = 'green';
    }

    document.body.setAttribute('id', theme);

    document.querySelector('.zhti_qiehuan_top span').innerText = themeMap[theme];

        const zhti_qiehuan = document.querySelector('.zhti_qiehuan');

            zhti_qiehuan.setAttribute('show', '0');

<script>

  let newHref = modifyDomain();
  let metaNode = document.createElement('meta');
  metaNode.setAttribute('http-equiv', 'mobile-agent');
  metaNode.setAttribute('content', 'format=html5;url='+ modifyDomain());
  document.head.append(metaNode);
  
  function modifyDomain() {
    var currentUrl = window.location.href;
    var domainParts = window.location.hostname.split('.');
   
    if (domainParts.length >= 3) {
        domainParts[0] = 'm';
    } else {
        domainParts.unshift('m');
    }
    var newDomain = domainParts.join('.');
    var newUrl = currentUrl.replace(window.location.hostname, newDomain);
  return newUrl;
}
</script>

<style>
/* 导航样式 */
.ching-xzmx-con-lb_p {
    color: red; /* 红色字体 */
    margin-top: -0.01em; /* 向上提半个字 */
}

/* 下拉菜单样式 */
.nav-item {
    position: relative; /* 为下拉菜单定位 */
    margin: 0 10px; /* 增加左右间距 */
}

.dropdown-menu {
    display: none; /* 默认隐藏 */
    position: absolute; /* 绝对定位 */
    background-color: #fff; /* 背景颜色 */
    border: 1px solid #ccc; /* 边框 */
    z-index: 10; /* 确保下拉菜单在上层 */
    padding: 0; /* 去掉内边距 */
    left: 50%; /* 使下拉菜单的左边距在父容器的中间 */
    transform: translateX(-50%); /* 使下拉菜单水平居中 */
    text-align: center; /* 居中对齐 */
}

/* 下拉菜单项样式 */
.dropdown-menu li {
    padding: 8px 12px; /* 内边距 */
    white-space: nowrap; /* 防止换行 */
}

/* 下拉菜单显示样式 */
.dropdown-menu li a {
    color: #000; /* 链接颜色 */
    text-decoration: none; /* 去掉下划线 */
    display: block; /* 链接全宽可点击 */
    padding: 8px 0; /* 上下内边距，确保点击区域足够大 */
    text-align: center; /* 居中对齐 */
    width: 100%; /* 链接占满父元素的宽度 */
}

/* 悬停时显示下拉菜单 */
.nav-item:hover .dropdown-menu {
    display: block; /* 鼠标悬停时显示下拉菜单 */
}

/* 移动端样式 */
@media (max-width: 768px) {
    .nav-item {
        cursor: pointer; /* 鼠标指针变为手型 */
    }

    .dropdown-menu {
        left: 0; /* 移动端不使用 transform */
        transform: none; /* 去掉 transform 属性 */
        width: 100%; /* 宽度设为 100% */
    }

    .dropdown-menu li a {
        text-align: center; /* 居中对齐 */
    }
}

</style>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // 获取下拉菜单项
    var dropdown = document.querySelector('.nav-item');
    var dropdownMenu = dropdown.querySelector('.dropdown-menu');

    // 鼠标进入时显示下拉菜单
    dropdown.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
        dropdownMenu.style.display = 'block';
    });

    // 鼠标离开时隐藏下拉菜单
    dropdown.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
        dropdownMenu.style.display = 'none';
    });

    // 移动端点击时切换下拉菜单显示
    dropdown.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
        event.stopPropagation(); // 阻止事件冒泡
        dropdownMenu.style.display = dropdownMenu.style.display === 'block' ? 'none' : 'block';
    });

    // 点击页面其他地方时隐藏下拉菜单
    document.addEventListener('click', function() {
        dropdownMenu.style.display = 'none';
    });
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

	if(/iPhone|iPod|iphone os|ipad/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
		zmkjfs();
	}

	function zmkjfs(){
		if (/(iPhone|iPad|iPod|iOS)/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
			if (isSafari()) {
				document.querySelector('.iosKJ').style.display = 'block';
			}
		} else if (/(Android)/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {

		}


	}
	function isSafari(){
		var ua = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
		if (ua.indexOf('applewebkit') > -1 && ua.indexOf('mobile') > -1 && ua.indexOf('safari') > -1 &&
				ua.indexOf('linux') === -1 && ua.indexOf('android') === -1 && ua.indexOf('chrome') === -1 &&
				ua.indexOf('ios') === -1 && ua.indexOf('browser') === -1) {
			return "Safari";
		}
		else {
			return "noSafari";
		}
	}

	document.querySelector('.iosKJ').addEventListener('click', function () {
		document.querySelector('.iosKJ').style.display = 'none';
	});


</script>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
       
        const list = document.querySelector('.list_content');
        const items = list.getElementsByTagName('a');
        const itemsToShowInitially = 10;


       
        let previousDate = '';
        let today = new Date();
        var tomorrow = new Date();
        tomorrow.setDate(today.getDate() + 1);

        function formatDate(date) {
            const year = date.getFullYear();
            const month = String(date.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
            const day = String(date.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
            return year + '-' + month + '-' + day;
        }

        var todayStr = formatDate(today);
        var tomorrowStr = formatDate(tomorrow);

      
        for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
           
            var item = items[i];
            var time = item.getAttribute('data-time');
            var date = new Date(time).toISOString().split('T')[0];
           
            if (date !== previousDate) {
                var dateHeader = document.createElement('p');
                dateHeader.className = 'date-p';
                let dateHeaderText = '';
                if (date === todayStr) {
                    dateHeaderText = '今日 ';
                } else if (date === tomorrowStr) {
                    dateHeaderText = '明日 ';
                }
                dateHeader.textContent = dateHeaderText + date;
                list.insertBefore(dateHeader, item);
                previousDate = date;
            }
        }

        const clickMoreNode = document.querySelector('.loadMoreBtn');
        clickMoreNode.addEventListener('click', function() {
            for (var i = itemsToShowInitially; i < items.length; i++) {
                items[i].style.display = 'block';
                (function (item) {
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        item.style.opacity = '1';
                    }, 50 * (i - itemsToShowInitially)); 
                })(items[i]);
            }
         
            clickMoreNode.style.display = 'none';
        })
    

    });
</script>

</body>
</html>
